    <script>/* eslint-disable */
(function (window, document) {

    function setCookie(key, value, domain, date) {
        document.cookie = key + '=' + encodeURIComponent(value) + ';domain=' + domain
            + ';path=/;expires=' + date.toGMTString() + ';';
    }

    var lsConf = window.lsConf;

    function excuteJS(code, version) {
        var head = document.head || document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        var scriptNode = document.createElement('script');
        scriptNode.dataset.version = version;
        scriptNode.appendChild(document.createTextNode(code));
        head.appendChild(scriptNode);
    }

    function excuteCss(code, version) {
        var head = document.head || document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        var styleNode = document.createElement('style');
        styleNode.type = 'text/css';
        styleNode.rel = 'stylesheet';
        styleNode.dataset.version = version;
        styleNode.appendChild(document.createTextNode(code));
        head.appendChild(styleNode);
    }

    function onError() {
        var date = new Date();
        setCookie(lsConf.lsVersionKey, '', document.domain || 'voice.baidu.com', date);
        window.location.reload();
    }

    function excuteLSCode(key, type) {
        try {
            var localStorage = window.localStorage;
            var code = localStorage.getItem(lsConf.lsPrefix + key);
            if (code.length <= 50) {
                onError();
                return;
            }
            if (type === 'js') {
                excuteJS(code, key);
            }
            else if (type === 'css') {
                excuteCss(code, key);
            }
        }
        catch (ex) {
            onError();
        }
    }
    window.excuteLSCode = excuteLSCode;

})(window, document);
</script>

<script>/* eslint-disable */
(function (window, document) {

    function setCookie(key, value, domain, date) {
        document.cookie = key + '=' + encodeURIComponent(value) + ';domain='
            + domain + ';path=/;expires=' + date.toGMTString() + ';';
    }

    var lsConf = window.lsConf;

    var date = new Date();
    var time = date.getTime();

    function error() {
        var domain = document.domain || 'voice.baidu.com';
        setCookie(lsConf.lsVersionKey, '', domain, date);
        setCookie(lsConf.lsSuportKey, 'no', domain, date);
    }

    var lsCodeKeyList = {}; /* 当前ls存储的完整keyList */
    var versionList = []; /* 当前需要存储的文件版本，用来放入cookie版本 */

    /* 获取已经从ls读取代码的版本列表 */
    [].forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.code-fr-ls'), function (item, index) {
        var version = item.getAttribute('data-version');
        versionList.push(version);
        lsCodeKeyList[lsConf.lsPrefix + version] = 1;
    });

    var localStorage = window.localStorage;
    try {
        if (localStorage) {
            var scripts = document.querySelectorAll('.code-to-write');
            [].forEach.call(scripts, function (script, index) {
                var version = script.getAttribute('data-version');
                var codeKey = lsConf.lsPrefix + version;
                lsCodeKeyList[codeKey] = 1;
                versionList.push(version);

                var code = script.textContent || script.innerText;
                localStorage.setItem(codeKey, code);

                /**
                 * 存储后看能否正常读到，不能读到说明对localStorage支持不够，设置不支持cookie
                 * 一般至少大于100长度才需要存储，单独的少于100就不要使用localStorage了
                 */
                if (localStorage.getItem(codeKey) === code) {
                    date.setTime(time + 604800000); /* 604800000 = 7 * 24 * 3600 * 1000 */
                    setCookie(lsConf.lsVersionKey, versionList.join('-'), document.domain, date);
                }
                else {
                    throw new Error('storage error');
                }
            });
        }
        /* 删除当前页面没有用的LSCode逻辑 */
        for (var key in localStorage) {
            if (key.indexOf(lsConf.lsPrefix) === 0 && lsCodeKeyList[key] !== 1) {
                localStorage.removeItem(key);
            }
        }
    }
    catch (ex) {
        error();
    }

})(window, document);
</script>
